SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-01-26 15:27:50') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-01-26 15:31:50') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-01-26 15:32:51') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-01-26 15:38:03') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-01-26 16:00:38') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-01-26 16:02:52') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-01-26 16:03:07') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-01-26 16:04:18') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-01-26 16:04:22') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-01-26 16:04:55') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-01-26 16:05:19') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-01-26 16:05:21') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-01-26 16:11:51') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-01-26 16:12:27') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-01-26 16:12:47') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-01-26 16:12:57') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-01-26 16:14:30') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-01-26 16:17:00') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-01-26 16:17:21') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-01-26 16:17:31') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-01-26 16:18:41') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-01-26 16:18:43') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-01-26 16:19:06') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-01-26 16:19:19') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-01-26 16:19:30') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-01-26 16:19:42') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-01-26 16:19:51') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-01-26 16:23:34') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-01-26 16:23:47') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-01-26 16:23:59') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-01-26 16:24:45') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-01-26 16:25:11') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-01-26 16:26:13') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-01-26 16:26:15') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC
